< Review>
If you like live musical theatre, you should give Performance Riverside a try. Landis Auditorium at RCC is a very nice venue.  The staging is well done. The lead performers are professionals and have excellent voices.  The tickets both single events and season are very reasonable. Performance Riverside is one of the little known gems of our city.<//Review>

We come here frequently, as it is my father in law's favorite restaurant. While I enjoy the vibe in the bar area, the dining room is pretty basic. The menu (especially breakfast) needs to be updated with some new and different options. I'm not a very big eater, but to me, the portions are quite small. The omlette and the huevos rancheros are tasty, but not enough to fill most people up. I love the throwback cocktails, and still enjoy coming here, but I  think it's getting a little tired and needs some fresh energy.< /Text>

< Text>
All donations are taken to a warehouse. People go in and select things that they need, but there is NO cost to them. They offer hit meals (donated by local restaurants) and have a food panty with donations from COSTCO. PLEASE HELP SUPPORT THEM.<//Text>
<Pics>None< /Pics><Resp>None< /Resp><gmapID>0x808fbb785fdfa671:0x1320b0756ef5e0ce<//gmapID></record>
</dataset><record>
< rating>
5< /rating>
< review>
I have been getting food at EHP for years. I am a senior living on SS. The food has improved significantly in the past year or two. They have partnered w/ Costco, Sprouts and Trader Joe's. Many delicious items including salads, sushi, vegetables, occasional meats, small prepared meals, pastries, cookies, cakes, yogurt-many about to out-date( they would have been discarded in the past).
They always have eggs, cooking oil, peanut butter, rice, beans, cereal, abundant breads, fresh bagels from a bagel shop, occasionally milk, yogurt, etc.
For the holidays, they have all the fixings. You choose either a roasting chicken or Turkey.
They are very organized and the staff are true humanitarians-low wages, hard work coordinating the food distribution, large donations, large deliveries of crates of fruits and vegetables. Jackie, Keesha, Suli, Opal(80 y.o. who has volunteered for 20 years), Nevida Butler, the founder of EHP years ago when they were on an extension of University Ave. known as "Whisky Gulch".

They also have a warehouse of household items (beds, vacuum cleaners, small space heaters,etc.) and clothing. You can put your name on a waiting list for certain items.
They appreciate donations and esp. folks volunteering a few hours every day.< /review>

<Date>1608324182576</Date>< review>
Nick the plumber from Canyon Hills Plumbing knew right away what he thought the problem was, with no hot water getting to only 1 shower.

It was the shower cartridge, and yes he could of sold me on a new shower valve body. But that would have entailed cutting drywall from the backside or cutting the portion of acrylic shower wall around the valve body and replace it, and would have been way more costly.

He replaced the cartridge which he had on his truck, and for a mere fraction of the cost the job was done within the hour. The cartridge was stuck in the valve body from over many years, and had become calcified in the body.  He worked diligently until it broke free and he got it out.

I found through the first experience with Canyon Hills Plumbing that I will use them again, if and when the need arises again.

Thank You Nick and Canyon Hills Plumbing for being reasonable and honest with your assessment of the work needed.

I had been to a different Sprint store earlier in the week and also had talked with Customer Care on the phone and both basically had said that I was going to pay $400 + up front to get a new phone.

< text>
So disappointed! On July 5th, I got tickets to a jazz show at Port City Sports Bar & Grill, scheduled July 10th, from 8-11 pm. My tickets were confirmed by EventBrite by email.

We drove down for the show and were parking, when I brought up my email program on my phone to have the ticket confirmation ready for admittance.

Imagine my surprise and dismay to receive an email that the event was postponed due to Covid-19. The email was date/time-stamped 7/10/20 @7:53pm.

Really?!? Send an email  a whole 7 MINUTES before the event was scheduled to start?!? This was supposed to have been our first outing since the "shelter at home" started in March.

I don't know if it was Port City or EventBrite that dropped the ball on this one. Either way, I was terribly disappointed.<//text>

< Text>
This place by far the best place, it has a nice set up. The food I order was really good as I expected. The noodle broth was well balance and has that nice soothing flavor, that's the first thing I do before I eat it. Is to taste the broth first to see how the flavor is before I eat the noodle. The spring roll was well nicely done, it was nice and fresh I can taste the freshness. The reason why gave it a (5 stars) Because as food critic there's things you look for when you dine in.

1). As you walk in how is the atmosphere and set up like.
2).Greeting and service.
3).The menu was nicely done.
4). Ordering was properly taken care of.
5). The food was really good and flavorful.

I order the special spring roll and spicy noodle (Bun Bo Hue) and my friend order the combination Pho noodle which he was complimenting how good it was on our way there. We were really satisfied. And I would really recommend it to friends and families if they're around the area. My next try is the (Hot Pot) .

#SupportingSmallBusiness</Text>
